# 护符项链

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：这是由浅绿色头发编程而成的漂亮颈环，中间镶嵌有一颗极其稀有的，经过附魔的红宝石。这是一名精灵弓箭手委托矮人打造的传奇饰品。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">被誉为最强半神的英雄，独自挑战、粉碎坠落的星星。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">据说从那之后，星星的命运就受到封印。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">碎星：佩戴者左右手各手持一把白刃武器时，可以选择其中一把武器作为主要武器，取该武器的武器基础属性、特殊属性和武器特性为武器底板，然后将另外一把武器的武器基础属性、特殊属性叠加到该武器上。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：镶有红色琥珀的链坠。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">琥珀为黄金树的古老露滴，在</font><font face="宋体">“初始艾尔登之王”葛孚雷的时代被视为特殊的宝石。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“传说中的护符”之一。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在黄金树尚未出现的史前时代，据说古龙是那时代的主宰，也是保护王的铜墙铁壁。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：以</font><font face="宋体">“艾尔登之王”拉达冈的形象制成的护符。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">“传说中的护符”之一。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">据说</font><font face="宋体">“红发”拉达冈，身为卡利亚的蕾娜菈的丈夫时，学习魔法；</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">身为玛莉卡女王的丈夫时，学习祷告</font><font face="宋体">──英雄的目标，是成为完美存在。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">红发英雄：每回合一次，佩戴者施展法术的动作下降一级（全回合动作</font><font face="宋体">-整轮动作-标准动作-移动动作-迅捷动作），最低降低为迅捷动作。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">王骑：佩戴者使用消耗关键属性包含心智系属性的能量的主动能力时，基础能耗降低</font><font face="宋体">3点，最低为1点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">狙击：佩戴者以弓箭进行特定部位攻击时，忽略特定部位攻击减值，并且以特定部位攻击造成的不良状态点数改为每造成</font><font face="宋体">1点伤害就造成1点不良状态点数，并且造成的不良状态点数可以叠加。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：以老旧锻造铁锤的形象制成的护符。表面刻着流纹文字。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">在远古时代，锻造是敬神的仪式。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">据说在熔化的钢铁中，一层层的皱褶内刻有文字。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">铁匠会找出文字，用于固定武器的灵魂。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：以双头剑与密使的形象制成的护符。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">密使们继承而来的双头剑剑术，贯彻攻击招招不致命，但最后一记攻击最为强力的作法。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">终结：佩戴者在施展多打类能力时，最后一次攻击若成功对目标造成伤害，则会对目标额外造成</font><font face="宋体">6点伤害，伤害类型与伤害级别与原本的伤害类型与伤害级别相同。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：护符</font> <font face="宋体">消耗品</font> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：</font><font face="宋体">1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">重量：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：当你佩带该玉佩时，若你处于死亡的危机之中，它将保护你一段时间。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">救命：当你受到任一伤害会使你死亡时，触发本效果，玉佩立即碎裂，你获得</font><font face="宋体">30点临时生命，持续时间为一个场景，或者被打空为止。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">当你受到任一即死效果时，若你会死亡，则你会立即免疫该效果，这会导致玉佩直接碎裂。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：护符</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：</font><font face="宋体">1</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：戴上它的持有者能够自行抵挡法术。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">物品特殊属性：【魔法】</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">魔法抵消：该护符每</font><font face="宋体">4小时会自动产生1点能量点，上限为6。当佩戴者受到法术时，该护符可以消耗能量点按照佩戴者的意愿决定是否抵挡该法术作用于佩戴者。若决定抵挡，则根据该法术的原本法术等级来决定结果：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">D级法术：该法术直接无效，消耗2点能量点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">C级法术：该法术直接无效，消耗3点能量点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">B级法术：该法术直接无效，消耗6点能量点。并且佩戴者进行一个1D10的机运检定，若结果不为成功，则护身符彻底摧毁。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">说明：若抵挡的法术为范围法术或者有多个目标，则只有作用佩戴者本身的效果被抵挡，其他目标照常生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">象征月亮，外形为拳头大小有水晶质感的银白色卧狼。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">灵敏嗅觉：你获得灵敏嗅觉。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">传奇感应：你获得相当于自身敏感范围一半的盲视，基于嗅觉。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">月之追猎：你花费一个标准动作，消耗</font><font face="宋体">1点意志力，你标记一个在你敏感范围内的目标，被你标记的目标能随时被你模糊定位，最大范围为感知值*1000米，持续24小时，你最多同时标记一个目标。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：当被标记的目标处于你本能力范围内时，若你无法通过正常的手段定位目标，通过本能力，你只是可以感知到其位置，但是其周边的情况，以及其当前在做什么这些信息，你完全不得而已。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个标记能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">魄影</font><font face="宋体">-乌鸦</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">本质：魔幻本质</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">C+1000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：护符</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：魄影是妖灵的身魄精华凝炼而成。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">象征不幸，外形为拳头大小有水晶质感的黑色展翅飞鸟。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">迅疾速奔：你的基础移动速度增加</font><font face="宋体">6米。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">黑色狡诈：当你敏感范围内有目标的生命值向下转化时（如【能量武器】特性，如攻击太阳穴等），无论其是原本的伤势还是本次受到的伤害，你都可以让其多转化</font><font face="宋体">4点，这4点在对应能力计算完毕后触发。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">如：特定攻击太阳穴，目标完全通过了豁免，没有生命值被恶化，则无法触发本能力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">重量：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：魄影是妖灵的身魄精华凝炼而成。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">象征祭祀，外形为拳头大小有水晶质感的乳白色羊头。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">完美意志：你的意志力池上限增加</font><font face="宋体">6点。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">祭祀象征：你每轮额外获得一个能且只能用于专注（引导）的标准动作（如常可以转化动作）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">礼祭天地：你每回合开始时，获得</font><font face="宋体">2点附加成功，该附加成功你可以将其分配在你本轮内进行的任何主动检定上，你必须在检定前先声明使用该附加成功。若不使用，则在本回合结束时，失去所有未使用的附加成功。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">绑定：要使用梅肯斯姆的力量，你必须将其佩戴在胸口（占据护符位）一个星期的时间，令其与你的生命气息同调。如果你取下了这块宝石，那么你需要再佩戴七天才能令其生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生命恢复：梅肯斯姆的佩戴者，以及其附近感知值</font><font face="宋体">/米内所有的友方单位自然恢复翻倍（短休若原本是1小时，现在变为15分钟，最低15分钟，长休若原本是8小时，现在变为2小时，最低2小时）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">快速医疗：佩戴者可以以一个标准动作激发宝石的力量，使感知值</font><font face="宋体">/米内的所有友方单位获得12点快速医疗，持续至目标的回合结束时。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：这是一块染血的宝石，内里包含着强烈的治愈力量。使用的时候需要支付与治疗相当的代价（血液），代价与伤口的程度成正比。除了即死以外的伤大部分都能治愈。</font>
</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生命复苏：死之转移在购买时会获得一共</font><font face="宋体">18点能量，以一个自由动作，每2点能量可以恢复1点恶性或者2点严重或者冲击伤害。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">邪恶吸取：死之转移的能量只能通过下述方式恢复：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">以一个整轮动作，对一个无助的生物使用，对其造成</font><font face="宋体">1点耐力伤害，恢复死之转移1点能量，吸血时宝石闪耀出非常不幸的血红之光，所以目睹吸血过程的人都会无条件将拥有者视作黑暗生物（但若你本身不是黑暗生物，那不会受那些本会影响黑暗生物的特性的影响），这可能会引发一些剧情效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">特殊：</font><font face="宋体">“邪恶吸取”只能吸收活体生物，植物，不死生物，构装体，灵体，虚体，以及没有血液的生物免疫死之转移的“邪恶吸取”效果。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">重量：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：以大盾与骑士的形象制成的护符。能提升防御强度。在过去，王城罗德尔的骑士们将大树守卫的准则奉为圭臬：善尽守护职责，该先举起的不是剑，是盾。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">守卫指责：当佩戴者处于格挡状态下时，每当佩戴者触及范围内有友方单位受到范围攻击，你可以选择使其针对该次攻击视为拥有全遮蔽，你自身照常豁免，若此次攻击为复数攻击，则你有可能受到</font><font face="宋体">2次攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">极限防御：当佩戴者处于格挡状态下时，每当佩戴者受到范围攻击时，若佩戴者豁免失败，则佩戴者可以选择该回合的如常受到伤害，但是该回合受到的所有范围伤害的最终伤害减半。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">每次长休佩戴者可以使用本能力的次数为佩戴者的传奇耐力</font><font face="宋体">/2次（最少1次）。本物品的能力无法与其他来源的类似效果叠加。当本物品处于冷却状态下，你无法卸下本装备。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">避劫：当装备者在一场战斗中对一个敌方目标至少进行了</font><font face="宋体">6次攻击行为并且全部命中后，本场战斗中若该敌方目标对装备者的一次攻击会导致装备者死亡，则装备者无视此次攻击，同时连带这次攻击附带的其他效果也一并无视。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：若装备者受到的是目标包含装备者的复数目标攻击，则装备者只会无视对自身进行的那一次攻击，不会影响其他目标。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：针对多段伤害类能力或者多次攻击，本效果只能无视触发的那一段，之前的所有效果依然有效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">C+1000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">分类：护符</font></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">体积：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">重量：忽略不计</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：我每日送他一尾金色鲤，他就与我袖传一课，依方位，百下百着。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">运气：装备者每次亲手击杀一个可以使自己获得支线奖励的目标后（这意味着难度至少要为</font><font face="宋体">“势均力敌”），可以投掷一个D10骰（这不是一次检定，不受任何改变掷骰结果的能力的影响，也不能重骰），若结果为10，则装备者立刻获得价值D+500的造物材料，可以被用于制造任何种类的装备。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：若</font><font face="宋体">ST不开放造物规则，则本物品直接被禁用，无需重复申明。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：本饰品进入冒险世界时就必须佩戴，并且必须佩戴完整一场，否则获得的奖励会立即失去，并且本物品无法被轮回之境回收。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
